As discussed at the erb meeting, attached you will find 3 documents
outlining our proposal for the HTML Object Model. This object model
supersets the existing functionality exposed by NS and IE. These
documents provide an outline of enhancements beyond the current NS and
IE model. I did not include detailed documentation describing current
behavior.


This document contains an overview of the HTML Object Model and
includes an overview of how to expose all the HTML elements and the HTML
text to the developer to allow completely interactive, dynamic pages to
be created.

This document contains an overview of an event bubbling architecture
that allows code to be generically written at various levels of the HTML
containership hierarchy.

This is a more detailed document describing how to manipulate the
document's content using a textRange object. With the textRange the
contents of the page can be modified after the page has been rendered,
without requiring any reloading of the document or any round-trips with
the server.

These are introductory documents. I am working on an IDL representation
for all the HTML Elements and the entire object hierarchy and will
submit those as soon as they are ready. In addition, I will try to have
documents describing current behavior sometime next week.

-Scott

begin 600 overview.htm
